 com / qkgbfokueb The festival of Bhai Dooj symbolizes the sacred relationship of brother and sister
 is din bahanen apane bhaaiyon kii khushi or lambii aayu ke liye mutyu ke devtaa yamraj kii puja karti hai
 What is the belief? It is believed that on this day Yamraj had seen his sister Yamuna
 yamuna ke swaagat se khush hokar yamraj ne vardaan diya tha ki is din jo bahanen apane bhaaiyon kii lambii aayu kii kaamana karke unke liye vrath rakhengi, tikaa karengi, to unke bhaaiyon kii raksha swany yamraj karenge
 It is also said that the brothers who get their sisters to eat tilak on this day and eat their handmade food, Yama Devta himself protects them
 bhai dooj 2017: bhaaiyon ke prati bahanon ke vishwaas kaa parv, jaane kab he muhuurtaaise karen yama devtaa kii upasna- shaam ko ghar ke baahar bain ore mitti ke kalash main jal bharkar rakhen
 - Burn a square lamp of mustard oil on it
 - phir prarthana karen ki ghar main rahane vaale sabhi log dderghaayu or swasth hon
 - Then sprinkle urn water in every corner of the house
 bhai dooj kaa mahatv:- diwali ke duusare din karthik shukla dwitiya ko bhai dooj kaa parv manaaya jaataa he
 On the day of Bhai Dooj, Chitragupta, the secretary of Yamraj is also worshiped
 - is tithi se yamraj or dwitiya tithi kaa sambandh hone ke kaaran isko yamadvitiya bhi kaha jaataa he
 On this day, the sisters greet their brother with tilak and welcome
 - saath hi apane bhai kii lambii aayu kii kaamana bhi karti hai
 That is why Bhai Dooj is celebrated, what is the mythological story? On the day of Bhai Dooj, the brothers should see the moon in the morning
 - iske baad yamuna ke jal se snaan karen yaa taaje jal se snaan karen
 - Then the brothers go to their sister's house and get food prepared by the sister's hands there
 - bahanen bhai ko bhojan karaaen or unka tilak karke aarti karen
 - Give the gift to your sister as brother wishes

 *** Today is the birthday of Tamil Nadu veteran late Kanjeevaram Natarajan Annadurai
 15 sitambar 1909 ko janme annadurai tamilnadu ke lokapriy netaa, apane pradesh ke pehle gaiyrcongressi mukhyamantri or dravid munnetra kadgam party ke sansthaapak the
 His name, 'anna', in short, means in Tamil, 'respected elder brother'
 unka janm ek behad saadhaaran parivaar main hua
 The story of modern Tamil Nadu is associated with this person of about five and a quarter feet five feet tall with tobacco, teeth, peeled beard and breathtaking dry voice
 annadurai apane bhaashanon ke liye bahut mashhoor the
 He was also a competent writer of Tamil language
 unhone na sirf kai naatak likhe, balki unamem abhinay bhi kiya
 Some of his plays were later made into films
 tamil cinema ko raajnneetik prachaar kaa astr banane waalon main unka naam pehla he
 Born into a normal family, Annadurai first worked as a school teacher, then soon came into the field of journalism
 vah hindi ke prabal virdohi or tamil bhashaa or sahitya ke pakke samarthak the
 He was a follower of Periyar EV Ramaswamy, the father of the Dravidian movement
 shuru main vah dravid kadgam ke sadsy the, par apane raajnneetik guru periyar se matbhed ke baad 1949 main vah dravid kadgam se alag ho gaye or apane sahyogiyon ke saath 'dravid munnetra kadgam' kii sthapana kii
 He gave a separate slogan of 'dravidanadu' for the Dravidians and resolved to end the Congress rule from the state
 annadurai kii shavyatra kii tasvirdravid munnetra kadgam ne apane lakshyon ke liye anek andolan kiye
 After ten years Annadurai finally took over the reins of the state
 haalanki asamyik mrityu ke chalate vah mukhyamantri kaarykaal ke do saal bhi puure nahin kar paae, lekin apane kaarykaal ke dauraan unhone tamil ke istemaal ko khub jor diya
 He is also credited with renaming the state of Madras as Tamil Nadu
 unki shavyatra main sabase zyada log shaamil hue or is baat ke liye ise 'ginis book of world records' main bhi shaamil kiya gaya
 When MG Ramachandran separated and formed his party in 1972, he named it Anna Dravida Munnetra Kazhagam after Annadurai
 tamilnadu kii maujuuda mukhyamantri jayalalita isi party kii adhyaksh hai
